Spades are permanent trumps: any card of the Spade suit beats any card of any other suit.\r\n\r\nCallBreak Multiplayer is a strategic trick-based card game. Deal and play are counter-clockwise. To succeed, a player must win the number of tricks called, or more trick than the call. If a player succeeds, the number called is added to his or her cumulative score. Otherwise the number called is subtracted.
